# Description __

Wood shutters that you can open and close.

# Sickle

# Description __

A very sharp curved cutting weapon. While its traditional role was to cut grass, this tool is also extremely versatile at cutting throats, perhaps trees, too.

Page views: 3,824  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Large Banner Hanging

# Description __

A large banner hanging on a wall.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x20 Cloth
  * x100 Metal Fragments



## Recycling Output __

  * x10 Cloth
  * x50 Metal Fragments

# Landscape Picture Frame

# Description __

A landscape oriented canvas for artists paintings. This items requires the [Sunburn Pack](/rust/sunburn) DLC to craft.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x100 Wood



## Recycling Output __

  * x50 Wood

# Large Banner on pole

# Description __

A large banner hanging on a pole.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x100 Wood
  * x50 Metal Fragments
  * x20 Cloth



## Recycling Output __

  * x50 Wood
  * x25 Metal Fragments
  * x10 Cloth

# Double Sign Post

# Description __

A double sign post that you can plant into terrain.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x75 Wood



## Recycling Output __

  * x38 Wood



Page views: 2,830  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Description __

A single sign post that you can plant into terrain.

# One Sided Town Sign Post

# Description __

A one sided town sign post, that you can plant into terrain.

Page views: 2,565  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Two Sided Town Sign Post

# Description __

A double sided town sign post, with roof, that you can plant into terrain.

Page views: 3,165  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Huge Wooden Sign

# Description __

A 6-meter by 3-meter wooden sign that you can write on. This is the largest sign available.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x250 Wood



## Recycling Output __

  * x125 Wood



Page views: 3,046  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Large Wooden Sign

# Description __

A 3-meter by 1.5-meter wooden sign that you can write on.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x150 Wood



## Recycling Output __

  * x75 Wood



Page views: 2,440  
Updated: This Year

# Description __

A 2-meter by 1-meter wooden sign that you can write on.

# Small Wooden Sign

# Description __

A 1-meter by 0.5-meter wooden sign that you can write on.

Page views: 2,526  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Skull Fire Pit

# Description __

Enjoy burning your enemies remnants to ashes with this Halloween exclusive! Provides warmth and light, and you can cook with it.

Page views: 3,408  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Sleeping Bag

# Description __

A sleeping bag. Placing this will give you a location to respawn.

Page views: 3,655  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Small Oil Refinery

# Description __

A small refinery which can produce Low Grade Fuel from Crude Oil.

Page views: 8,823  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Small Water Bottle

# Description __

A Small Water Bottle. Left click to drink, right click to fill from water sources, or to pour out.

Page views: 2,599  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Custom SMG

# Description __

A rapid-firing Machine Gun. Sacrifices accuracy and distance for speed.

Page views: 8,341  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [MP5A4](/rust/item/smg.mp5)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/smg.mp5)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/smg.mp5~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/smg.mp5~history)



# MP5A4

# Description __

This sub machinegun has the highest damage of the it's class but also has the highest recoil. Highly effective in short-medium ranges in the hands of a skilled shooter.

  
  
  
  
  
  


# General Information __

The MP5A4 can be crafted at a level 2 workbench using the following materials:

Material | Quantity  
---|---  
High-Quality Metal | 50  
Gears | 20  
Metal Springs | 10  
SMG Body | 1  
  
The MP5A4 can also be found rarely in loot crates, as well as in the hands of certain NPCs like the Military Tunnels scientists and the Heavy Scientists at the Oil Rig. It can also be purchased from the Bandit Camp for 750 Scrap.

The MP5A4 can be loaded with 30 rounds of 9mm ammunition and is compatible with a range of attachments, including scopes, muzzle attachments, and magazines.

## Damage and Durability __

The MP5A4 deals 25 damage per hit to players and has a durability of 200.

## Attachment Compatibility __

The MP5A4 is compatible with the following attachments:

  * Muzzle: 
    * Muzzle Brake
    * Silencer
    * Flash Hider
  * Sight: 
    * Holosight
    * 8x Zoom Scope
    * Simple Handmade Sight
    * 16x Zoom Scope
    * 4x Zoom Scope
    * 2x Zoom Scope
    * Laser Sight
  * Magazine: 
    * 30-Round Magazine



## Interesting Facts __

  * The MP5A4 is based on the real-life MP5 submachine gun.
  * The MP5A4 has been a popular choice for players in Rust due to its high damage and versatility in close-to-medium range combat.



The MP5A4 is a highly sought-after weapon in Rust, with its high damage output and compatibility with a range of attachments making it a formidable weapon in the right hands. While it can be difficult to control due to its high recoil, skilled shooters can make the most of its potential in combat.

# Thompson

# Description __

A medium damage sub machine gun effective at short ranges.

Page views: 8,157  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# SMG Body

# Description __

The firing mechanism of a submachinegun. Used in construction of a weapon that can fire pistol ammo fully automatic.

Page views: 4,709  
Updated: A Long Time Ago
